Hi all,
Like what I did for 0.3.1, this experimental code is very urgly for SWD
support.
And it's only used for test purpose.
I test it OK on STM32 and LPC1700.
Attached also is the -d3 output when operating STM32 and LPC1700.
People can compare it with output when using JTAG.
Hope it can be helpful for SWD support in OpenOCD.

-- 
Best Regards, SimonQian
http://www.SimonQian.com
